SDK API Guide  Version 6.5.18
SOC Properties
SOC Properties
Define Property Type Default Description
spn_STATION_MAC_ADDRESS station_mac_address String 00:00:00:00:01:00 Station MAC address used for management through the switch ports itself. If using the CPU network interface, the NVRAM setting is used for MAC address assignment.
spn_POLLED_IRQ_MODE polled_irq_mode 0 Enable polled IRQ mode (useful for board bringup and debugging). IRQs will be polled from a dedicated thread and hardware interrupts will remain disabled.
spn_POLLED_IRQ_DELAY polled_irq_delay IPOLL_THREAD_DELAY The priority of the IRQ poll thread as well as the minimum delay between IRQ polls can be configured if needed.
spn_POLLED_IRQ_PRIORITY polled_irq_priority IPOLL_THREAD_PRIO The priority of the IRQ poll thread as well as the minimum delay between IRQ polls can be configured if needed.
spn_FILTER_ENABLE filter_enable 1 Allow filtering to be disabled in hardware if not being used. Also, tables will not be cleared which can save time in simulation.
spn_BCM_NUM_COS bcm_num_cos (tme==1 Initial number of CoS queues bcm_init() configures the chip for.
spn_BCM_FILTER_CLEAR_FE bcm_filter_clear_fe 1 Clear the filter table for 10/100Mb ports during initialization
spn_BCM_FILTER_CLEAR_GE bcm_filter_clear_ge 1 Clear the filter table for 1000Mb ports during initialization
spn_BCM_FILTER_CLEAR_XE bcm_filter_clear_xe 1 Clear the filter table for 10GE ports during initialization
spn_BCM_LINKSCAN_PBMP bcm_linkscan_pbmp String Linkscan: Specify ports on which bcm_init will run linkscan (default all).
spn_BCM_LINKSCAN_INTERVAL bcm_linkscan_interval 250000 Linkscan interval in microseconds. If non-zero, bcm_init() will start linkscan
spn_BCM_LINKSCAN_MAXERR bcm_linkscan_maxerr Port 5 The number of port update errors which will cause the bcm_linkscan module to suspend a port from update processing for the period of time set in "bcm_linkscan_errdelay".
spn_BCM_LINKSCAN_ERRDELAY bcm_linkscan_errdelay Port 10000000 The amount of time in microseconds for which the bcm_linkscan module will suspend a port from further update processing after "bcm_linkscan_maxerr" errors are detected. After this delay, the error state for the port is cleared and normal linkscan processing resumes on the port.
spn_BCM_STAT_PBMP bcm_stat_pbmp String BCM Statistics Collection: Set bitmap of ports on which stat collection will be enabled. Default is all ports.
spn_INT_LINK_METADATA_PBMP int_link_metadata_pbmp String INT per port metadata collection: Set bitmap of ports for which link metadata collection will be enabled in the uKernel.
spn_BCM_STAT_INTERVAL bcm_stat_interval interval Set stat collection interval in microseconds. Setting this to 0 will prevent counters from being started.
spn_BCM_STAT_SYNC_TIMEOUT bcm_stat_sync_timeout 10000000 Timeout delay in microseconds before bcm_stat_sync returns BCM_E_TIMEOUT
spn_BCM_STAT_FLAGS bcm_stat_flags COUNTER_FLAGS_DEFAULT Flag values to be ORd together: 0x0 indicates that counter DMA should NOT be used 0x1 indicates that counter DMA should be used (default).
spn_BCM_STAT_JUMBO bcm_stat_jumbo 1518 Threshold value for oversize (*OVR) frame size. Values over 1518 affect the *OVR statistics computation
spn_CAUI_RX_CLOCK_RECOVERY_LANE caui_rx_clock_recovery_lane 0 Selection of recovery clock lane for CAUI port. values: 0-3
spn_PREAMBLE_SOP_ONLY preamble_sop_only FALSE Specified if port use 1 Byte preamble
spn_BCM_TX_THREAD_PRI bcm_tx_thread_pri DEFAULT_TX_PRI Specifies the priority of the BCM TX thread
spn_BCM_RX_THREAD_PRI bcm_rx_thread_pri RX_THREAD_PRI_DFLT Specifies the priority of the BCM RX thread
spn_RX_POOL_NOF_PKTS rx_pool_nof_pkts BCM_RX_POOL_COUNT_DEFAULT Specifies number of packets for BCM RX buffer allocation. This is equal to number of channels x chains per channel x descriptors per chain. For multi unit systems, the resulting value needs to be multiplied by number of units.
spn_LINKSCAN_THREAD_PRI linkscan_thread_pri 50 Specifies the priority of the BCM Linkscan thread
spn_PORTMON_THREAD_PRI portmon_thread_pri 50 Specifies the priority of the BCM Portmon thread
spn_BST_SYNC_THREAD_PRI bst_sync_thread_pri 50 Specifies the priority of the bcm_bst_sync_thread
spn_BHH_THREAD_PRI bhh_thread_pri BHH_THREAD_PRI_DFLT Specifies the priority of the bcmBHH thread
spn_IBOD_SYNC_THREAD_PRI ibod_sync_thread_pri 50 Specifies the priority of the bcmIbodSync thread
spn_BCM_FT_REPORT_THREAD_PRI bcm_ft_report_thread_pri 50 Specifies the priority of the bcmFtExportDma thread
spn_BFD_THREAD_PRI bfd_thread_pri BCM_ESW_BFD_THREAD_PRI_DFLT Specifies the priority of the bcmBFD thread
spn_SOC_DMA_MONITOR_THREAD_PRI soc_dma_monitor_thread_pri 0 Specifies the priority of the dma monitor thread thread(bcmDmaIntrM)
spn_SOC_KNET_RX_THREAD_PRI soc_knet_rx_thread_pri 0 Specifies the priority of the SOC KNET RX thread
spn_BCM_ESW_PSCAN_THREAD_PRI bcm_esw_pscan_thread_pri BCM_ESW_PSCAN_THREAD_PRI_DFLT Specifies the priority of the bcmPSCAN thread
spn_SBUS_DMA_DESC_THREAD_PRI sbus_dma_desc_thread_pri 50 Specifies the priority of the socdmadesc thread
spn_ESM_RECOVERY_THREAD_PRI esm_recovery_thread_pri 50 Specifies the priority of the esm_recovery thread
spn_PDMA_TIMEOUT_USEC pdma_timeout_usec 500000 Packet DMA abort timeout
spn_CDMA_TIMEOUT_USEC cdma_timeout_usec 10000000 Counter DMA collection pass timeout in microseconds
spn_CDMA_PIO_HOLD_ENABLE cdma_pio_hold_enable 1 Manually collect the HOLD register in the counter DMA thread on BCM568xx and BCM567xx devices.
spn_TDMA_TIMEOUT_USEC tdma_timeout_usec soc->tableDmaTimeout Table DMA operation timeout in microseconds
spn_TDMA_INTR_ENABLE tdma_intr_enable 1 Table DMA operation should use interrupt rather than poll for completion
spn_TSLAM_TIMEOUT_USEC tslam_timeout_usec soc->tslamDmaTimeout Table SLAM DMA operation timeout in microseconds
spn_TSLAM_INTR_ENABLE tslam_intr_enable 1 Table SLAM DMA operation should use interrupt rather than poll for completion
spn_SCHANFIFO_TIMEOUT_USEC schanfifo_timeout_usec soc->schanFifoTimeout SCHAN FIFO operation timeout in microseconds
spn_SCHANFIFO_INTR_ENABLE schanfifo_intr_enable 1 SCHAN FIFO operation should use interrupt rather than poll for completion
spn_CCMDMA_TIMEOUT_USEC ccmdma_timeout_usec soc->ccmDmaTimeout CCM DMA operation timeout in microseconds
spn_CCMDMA_INTR_ENABLE ccmdma_intr_enable 1 CCM DMA operation should use interrupt rather than poll for completion
spn_DMA_DESC_TIMEOUT_USEC dma_desc_timeout_usec soc->sbd_dm_inf->timeout SBUSDMA descriptor mode operation timeout in microseconds
spn_DMA_ABORT_TIMEOUT_USEC dma_abort_timeout_usec 0 timeout for DMA abort (of all DMA types) in microseconds
spn_DMA_DESC_INTR_ENABLE dma_desc_intr_enable 1 SBUSDMA descriptor mode operation should use interrupt rather than poll for completion
spn_DCB_INTR_MITIGATE_ENABLE dcb_intr_mitigate_enable 0 Packet DMA interrupts should be mitigated to improve performance
spn_SOC_CTR_MAXERR soc_ctr_maxerr 5 Maximum number of consecutive S-channel errors the counter collection code will tolerate before the counter thread gives up and exits.
spn_SOC_COUNTER_CONTROL_LEVEL soc_counter_control_level HIGH_LEVEL stat info will include the specific priotity and higher priorities possible values: LOW_LEVEL, MEDIUM_LEVEL, HIGH_LEVEL.
spn_SOC_SKIP_RESET soc_skip_reset 0 Skip hardware reset (CMIC_CONFIG.RESET_CPS) when calling soc_reset(). This means that e.g. 'init soc' will NOT perform a hard reset.
spn_COUNTER_THREAD_PRI counter_thread_pri 50 Miscellaneous thread priorities; 0 is highest and 255 is lowest
spn_COUNTER_EVICT_THREAD_PRI counter_evict_thread_pri 50 Miscellaneous thread priorities; 0 is highest and 255 is lowest
spn_COUNTER_EVICT_HOSTBUF_SIZE counter_evict_hostbuf_size 8192 Number of entries in host buffer used for FIFO DMA in counter eviction
spn_COUNTER_EVICT_ENTRIES_MAX counter_evict_entries_max 0 Number of entries in host buffer after which eviction thread should yield
spn_CB_ABORT_ON_ERR cb_abort_on_err 0 Check callback return code and abort on error.
spn_LCCDRAIN_TIMEOUT_USEC lccdrain_timeout_usec 250000 When a link goes down for any reason, the driver waits for all packets to that port to drain from the MMU before continuing. There is a timeout in case the packet count is non-zero AND non-decrementing. This is only for devices with UniMAC and TriMAC.
spn_SOC_SCOREBOARD_ENABLE soc_scoreboard_enable 0
spn_SOC_SCOREBOARD_INTERVAL soc_scoreboard_interval 2000000
spn_L3_ENABLE l3_enable 1 L3 switching enable
spn_IPMC_ENABLE ipmc_enable 1 IMPC switching enable
spn_IPMC_DO_VLAN ipmc_do_vlan 1 Include the VLAN as part of the hash key for L3 IPMC
spn_IPMC_L2_USE_VLAN_VPN ipmc_l2_use_vlan_vpn 0 Enable broadcast domain (VLAN/VPN) hash keys lookup for L2 IPMC In absence of this config the device loopkup IPMC multicast table based on L3 ingress interface.
spn_TRUNK_EXTEND trunk_extend 1 EXTEND maximum number of front panel trunk groups from 32 to 128
spn_ARL_RESYNC_DELAY arl_resync_delay 3000000 Delay this long after an ARL message overrun before a lengthy ARL- resync process. Setting to 0 to disables resync, in peril of getting an inconsistent ARL message stream and/or corrupt L2 shadow table.
spn_L2XMSG_AVL l2xmsg_avl 1 on most XGS devices, 0 on BCM5660x Enable L2X shadowing into AVL tree.
spn_L2XMSG_MODE l2xmsg_mode L2MODE_POLL Mode control to select L2 Table DMA mode aka L2MODE_POLL (0) or L2MOD_FIFO mechanism aka L2MODE_FIFO (1) for L2 table change notification.
spn_L2XMSG_THREAD_PRI l2xmsg_thread_pri 50 Priority of the soc_l2x_thread, that is used to synchronize shadow copy of the L2 entry with the HW table
spn_L2XMSG_THREAD_USEC l2xmsg_thread_usec 3000000 Period between synchronizations of the software L2X shadow table with the hardware (5690 only). The thread actually runs every l2xmsg_thread_usec/l2xmsg_chunks microseconds.
spn_L2XMSG_SHADOW_HIT_BITS l2xmsg_shadow_hit_bits 1 The l2xmsg thread will call back to the user any time an L2X address is added, removed, or changed. However, if only the hit bit changes, it will not call back unless l2xmsg_shadow_hit_bits is set to 1.
spn_L2XMSG_SHADOW_HIT_SRC l2xmsg_shadow_hit_src 0 The l2xmsg thread will call back to the user any time an L2X address is added, removed, or changed. However, if only the source hit bit changes, it will not call back unless l2xmsg_shadow_hit_bits is set to 0 and l2xmsg_shadow_hit_src is set to 1.
spn_L2XMSG_SHADOW_HIT_DST l2xmsg_shadow_hit_dst 0 The l2xmsg thread will call back to the user any time an L2X address is added, removed, or changed. However, if only the destination hit bit changes, it will not call back unless l2xmsg_shadow_hit_bits is set to 0 and l2xmsg_shadow_hit_dst is set to 1.
spn_L2XMSG_CHUNKS l2xmsg_chunks 8 Synchronize the L2X table in chunks to spread out the work over time and save memory on size of DMA buffer. Must be power of 2.
spn_L2XMSG_HOSTBUF_SIZE l2xmsg_hostbuf_size 1024 Size of the buffer that is used to drain L2 FIFO when working in the L2 FIFO mode
spn_ARL_CLEAN_TIMEOUT_USEC arl_clean_timeout_usec 5000000 Timeout for hardware-accelerated ARL delete operations including: delete by port, delete by port+modid, delete by VLAN, delete by trunk.
spn_MEM_SCAN_THREAD_PRI mem_scan_thread_pri 50 Specifies the priority of the memory scanning and error correction thread
spn_MEM_SCAN_CHUNK_SIZE mem_scan_chunk_size 256 Specifies the number of table entries to be retrieved at a time during memory scanning.
spn_MEM_SCAN_ENABLE mem_scan_enable 1 Control to automatically run background memory scan.
spn_MEM_SCAN_RATE mem_scan_rate 4096 Specifies the memory scan rate in terms of entries per pass.
spn_MEM_SCAN_INTERVAL mem_scan_interval 10000000 Specifies the memory scan repeat interval.
spn_MEM_SCAN_NON_TCAM_ITERATIONS mem_scan_non_tcam_iterations 2 Specifies how many non-TCAM cycles to perform for every complete TCAM sweep in memscan.
spn_SRAM_SCAN_THREAD_PRI sram_scan_thread_pri 50 Specifies the priority of the sram scanning and error correction thread
spn_SRAM_SCAN_CHUNK_SIZE sram_scan_chunk_size 256 Specifies the number of table entries to be retrieved at a time during sram scanning.
spn_SRAM_SCAN_ENABLE sram_scan_enable 0 Control to automatically run background sram scan.
spn_SRAM_SCAN_RATE sram_scan_rate 4096 Specifies the sram scan rate in terms of entries per pass.
spn_SRAM_SCAN_INTERVAL sram_scan_interval 100000000 Specifies the sram scan repeat interval.
spn_SCHAN_TIMEOUT_USEC schan_timeout_usec soc->schanTimeout S-Channel operation timeout in microseconds. Note that ARL insert/delete messages can take a while if the ARL is highly active.
spn_MIIM_TIMEOUT_USEC miim_timeout_usec soc->miimTimeout MIIM operation timeout in microseconds
spn_BIST_TIMEOUT_MSEC bist_timeout_msec soc->bistTimeout Memory Built-In-Self-Test (BIST) timeout in milliseconds
spn_SCHAN_INTR_ENABLE schan_intr_enable 1 Normally, the system will use polling for register/memory S-Channel operations and interrupts for time-consuming operations such as ARL insert/delete. If this schan_intr_enable is set to 0, polling will be used for ALL operations.
spn_SCHAN_ERROR_BLOCK_USEC schan_error_block_usec 250000 Length of time to block the S-Channel error interrupt after one occurs. Prevents monopolizing the CPU (use 0 to disable any blocking).
spn_MIIM_INTR_ENABLE miim_intr_enable 1 If miim_intr_enable variable is set to 1, the system will use interrupts for MII operations since they take a while (70 usec or so). If this variable is set to 0, polling will be used for all MII operations.
spn_ARL_RATE_LIMIT arl_rate_limit 3000 Limit the number of ARL messages/sec the software will process, to keep it from hogging the CPU. Set to 0 to disable. Does not apply to L2X shadow table (see l2xmsg_thread_usec instead).
spn_MMU_SDRAM_ENABLE mmu_sdram_enable 1 MMU SDRAM configuration
spn_DIAG_LB_PACKET_TIMEOUT diag_lb_packet_timeout 5 Diagnostics loopback (tr 17 through tr 24) timeout in seconds for loopback packet reception
spn_DIAG_LB_FILL_RX diag_lb_fill_rx 0 Diagnostics loopback - if set to TRUE, all receive buffers are filled with 0xdeadbeef before DMAing into them. It is slow, but then you will know if loopback miscompares are due to skipped PCI writes.
spn_DIAG_PW_THREAD_PRI diag_pw_thread_pri 100 Packet watcher thread priority
spn_DIAG_PW_BUFFER_SIZE diag_pw_buffer_size -1 When set to >= 68, packet watcher will run in truncating mode, allocating smaller Rx buffers and accepting oversized packets on all Rx DMA channels.
spn_CFAP_TESTS cfap_tests MT_PAT_CHECKER|MT_PAT_ICHECKER Select memory tests run by cfapinit (default MT_PAT_FIVES and MT_PAT_AS)
spn_PHY_ENABLE phy_enable 1 If phy_enable is set to 0, all ports will use the null PHY driver. This is useful for simulations on Quickturn.
spn_PHY_NULL phy_null Port 0 If phy_null<port> is set to 1, the port will use the null PHY driver. This is useful for configuring direct-connect GMII links such as the chip-to-chip links on a 48-port board (example shown for 48 port board).
spn_PHY_SIMUL phy_simul Port 0 If phy_simul_<port> is set to 1, the port will use the simulation.
spn_PHY_AUTOMEDIUM phy_automedium Port 1 Fiber vs. copper autodetection enable.
spn_PHY_FIBER_PREF phy_fiber_pref Port 1 Fiber vs. copper preference When automedium is enabled, phy_fiber_pref indicates which medium to prefer if BOTH are active. Selects fiber (1) or copper (0). When automedium is disabled, phy_fiber_pref indicates which medium to use. Selects fiber (1) or copper (0).
spn_PHY_FIBER_DEGLITCH_USECS phy_fiber_deglitch_usecs Port 0 Fiber de-glitch: some GBICs may cause a brief fiber energy detect when inserted, even without a link. This could cause the copper link to be dropped, so an energy detect de-glitch is provided. The phy_fiber_deglitch_usecs is the de-glitch time in usec. This is only applied to BCM5421S PHY device.
spn_PHY_AUTONEG_TIMEOUT phy_autoneg_timeout Port 250000 Per-port parameter on maximum time to wait for PHY autoneg busy condition.
spn_PHY_SERDES phy_serdes
spn_PHY_SERDES_AUTOS phy_serdes_autos Port 0 Serdes Autonegotiation configuration This per-port parameter specifies what will happen if autonegotiation is on but the remote partner is not autonegotiating. If the value is zero, we will not link. If the value is non-zero, we will link.
spn_PHY_5464S phy_5464S Port 0 This specifies the external PHY device is BCM5464S.
spn_PHY_5690 phy_5690 Port FALSE This specifies the external PHY device is BCM5690.
spn_PHY_8706 phy_8706 Port FALSE This specifies the external PHY device is BCM8706 and equivalent.
spn_PHY_8072 phy_8072 Port FALSE This specifies the external PHY device is BCM8072 and equivalent.
spn_PHY_84740 phy_84740 Port FALSE This specifies the external PHY device is BCM84740.
spn_PHY_84752 phy_84752 Port FALSE This specifies the external PHY device is BCM84752.
spn_PHY_84753 phy_84753 Port FALSE This specifies the external PHY device is BCM84753.
spn_PHY_84754 phy_84754 Port FALSE This specifies the external PHY device is BCM84754.
spn_PHY_84064 phy_84064 Port FALSE This specifies the external PHY device is BCM84064.
spn_PHY_CHAIN_LENGTH phy_chain_length Port FALSE This specifies the position of external phy in the phy chain.
spn_XPHY_PRIMARY_CORE_NUM xphy_primary_core_num Port FALSE This specifies the primary core number to which it belongs to.
spn_PHY_TOPOLOGY phy_topology Port 0xFF:-1:-1

This specifies the position of external phy in the phy chain. For Recent PHY devices, logical ports can span across multiple cores These cores could be connected to multi-core external PHYs or Single core multi-lane external PHYs This presents complex topology options. Here is the format of the new config variable: Format1: phy_topology_pport_xphyId=mdio-addr:sys_lane:line_lane Format2: phy_topology_pport_xphyId_mapX=mdio-addr:sys_lane:line_lane where: pport = physical port number xphyId = position of the external PHY in the chain mdio_addr = mdio address of the external phy sys_lane = system side physical lane number line_lane = line side physical lane number mapX = index of lane mapping for specific pport and xphyId The above mentioned config would help in figuring out the physical lane numbers associated with the logical port to enable programming where there is no logical to logical lane mapping Here is an example for format1 case that show multiple cores connected to a external phy and it corresponding topology config

________
________
CORE0 EXTPHY
________
________
________

| | Sys side | | ________ | | | | | | Line side | |\ | |__________ | | \ | | | CORE0 |\ \ /| |__________ | | \ \ / | | | |\ \ \/ /| |__________ | | \ \/\/ | | |________|\ \/\/\/| |__________ \/\/\/| | ________ /\/\/\ | | | |/ /\/\ | | | | / /\ \ | | | |/ / \ | | | CORE0 | / \ | EXTPHY | | |/ | | | | | | | |________| | |________| |________|

In the above image the physical lane swap crossed the core boundary on core1&2 and there is no logical to logical mapping for lanes 4 to 11 on the system side of ExtPhy with the internal PHY. If the user wants to run the PRBS on logical lane 4 (on internal PHY core1 logical lane 0), the driver can query the DB and get the necessary physical lane information (physical lane 8 in this case). Here is an example for format2 case that show the mux mode that one core connects to a external phy and it corresponding topology config

| | ________ | |__________ | |________| |__________\ | | | |__________ - PORT1 | |________| |__________/ | | | | | CORE | | EXTPHY | | |________| |__________ | | | |__________\ | |________| |__________ - PORT2 |________| | |__________/ | | |________| Sys side Line side

In the above image, port1 and port2 map 4 line lanes and 2 system lines. There is no logical to logical mapping for lanes 0 to 7 on the system side of ExtPhy with the internal PHY. Here is an example to describe the relation. The format just describes the lane bitmap related with the port. Port1: mdio-addr is supposed to 0x10 and the first physical port is supposed to 0x8 phy_topology_8_1_map1=0x10:0:0 phy_topology_8_1_map2=0x10:0:1 phy_topology_9_1_map1=0x10:1:2 phy_topology_9_1_map2=0x10:1:3 Port2: phy_topology_10_1_map1=0x10:1:4 phy_topology_10_1_map2=0x10:1:5 phy_topology_11_1_map1=0x10:1:6 phy_topology_11_1_map2=0x10:1:7

spn_PHY_LANE0_L2P_MAP phy_lane0_l2p_map Port 0 Specify the physical lane number corresponding to the logical lane0 .
spn_PHY_AN_C72 phy_an_c72 Port FALSE This controls the clause 72 enable(1), disable(0).
spn_PHY_AN_FEC phy_an_fec Port FALSE This controls the clause 91(FEC) enable(2), the clause 74(FEC) enable(1), disable(0).
spn_PHY_EXT_AN_FEC phy_ext_an_fec Port 0 Advertise Clause 74 (or) Clause 91 Forward Error Correction (FEC) as part of Auto-Negotiation ability for external PHYs 0 - Do not advertise FEC as Auto-Negotiation ability. 1 - Advertise FEC CL74 as Auto-Negotiation ability. 2 - Advertise FEC CL91 as Auto-Negotiation ability.
spn_PHY_AN_C73 phy_an_c73 Port FALSE This controls the clause 73 auto-negotiation. Disable cl73(0), Enable cl73_and_c73bam(1), Enable cl73_wo_c73bam(2), Enable cl73_and_MSA(3), Enable MSA_ONLY(4). Enable CL73_CL37(5).
spn_PHY_AN_C37 phy_an_c37 Port FALSE This controls the clause 37 auto-negotiation. Disable cl37(0), Enable cl37_and_c37bam(1), Enable cl37_wo_c37bam(2).
spn_PHY_AN_ALLOW_PLL_CHANGE phy_an_allow_pll_change Port FALSE This controls if pll change allowed during AN enable(1), disable(0).
spn_SERDES_AN_C73_TX_FIFO_RESET_ENABLE serdes_an_c73_tx_fifo_reset_enable Port FALSE This config enables TX FIFO RESET routine in Warpcore firmware. The routine performs a targeted reset of the tx_os8_fifo whenever the CL73 arbitration FSM enters either the TX_DISABLE or the AN_GOOD_CHECK states. When enabled this config applies to independent channel mode when CL73 AN is enabled. The config is relevant to Warpcore B0/C0/.. By default, the routine is disabled in firmware.
spn_PHY_EXT_ROM_BOOT phy_ext_rom_boot Port 1 This controls whether to load the external ROM microcode to the applicable PHY devices, load(1), not load(0).
spn_PHY_FORCE_FIRMWARE_LOAD phy_force_firmware_load Port 1 This controls whether to force firmware load during PHY init of applicable PHY devices, auto load (2) force load (1), may skip load(0) This is also used for specifying download method. Along with force(1) 2nd nibble is used to specify firmware download method. Below are the values for firmware download methods 0x01 Do not download the firmware 0x11 force download the FW through MDIO 0x21 force download(Flash) FW to EEPROM 0x12 auto download the FW throgh MDIO if the version is not same as current one.
spn_PHY_LONG_XFI phy_long_xfi Port 1 This indicates whether the long cable is used on the external PHY device with XFI interface, By default XFI cannot drive long distance cables. TX preemphasis needs to be adjusted if long cables are used on the XFI side.
spn_PHY_HALF_POWER phy_half_power Port 0 this controls half power mode for applicable PHY devices, enable(1), disable(0).
spn_PHY_LOW_POWER_MODE phy_low_power_mode Port 7 set BCM5488 family PHY to operate in class A/B low power mode. Accept value 0(lowest power) to 7(highest power).
spn_PHY_OCTAL_PORT_FIRST phy_octal_port_first Port 0 indicate which port is the first port of the octal PHY.
spn_PHY_HL65_1LANE_MODE phy_hl65_1lane_mode Port xgxs_ctrl Set the given XGXS control mode in independent channel mode for Hyperlite/Hypercore/Warpcore serdes. Valid value 4,5, and 6
spn_PHY_8040_SWITCH_PORT phy_8040_switch_port Port PHY8040_DFLT_SWITCH_PORT Specify switch port on BCM8040. The switch port is the port connecting to MAC side device.
spn_PHY_8040_MUX_PORT0 phy_8040_mux_port0 Port PHY8040_DFLT_MUX_PORT0 Specify mux port0 on BCM8040. A mux port will connect to another PHY device.
spn_PHY_8040_MUX_PORT1 phy_8040_mux_port1 Port PHY8040_DFLT_MUX_PORT1 Specify mux port1 on BCM8040. A mux port will connect to another PHY device.
spn_PHY_8040_MUX_PORT2 phy_8040_mux_port2 Port PHY8040_MUX_PORT_INVALID Specify mux port2 on BCM8040. A mux port will connect to another PHY device. The port is treated as invalid if there is no PHY device connecting to
spn_PHY_53314_CLK156 phy_53314_clk156 1 Specify 53314 PHY device operating frequency as 156.25MHz.
spn_PHY_BUS_I2C phy_bus_i2c Port 0 Specify the external PHY device uses I2C bus instead of MDIO bus
spn_PHY_COPPER_SFP phy_copper_sfp Port 0 Specify the external PHY device is a copper SFP PHY
spn_PHY_FIBER_CAPABLE phy_fiber_capable Port 1 The PHY has a fiber medium in addition to a copper medium
spn_PHY_OPERATIONAL_MODE phy_operational_mode Port 0 Set phy operational mode (repeater/retimer/Gearbox/EBE). Value 0 => Repeater (default) Value 1 => Retimer Value 2 => Gearbox Value 3 => EBE
spn_PHY_INIT_CL72 phy_init_cl72 Port FALSE Initialize external phy with CL72 enabled
spn_PHY_ALT_DATAPATH_MODE phy_alt_datapath_mode Port 0 Set phy datapath mode (default/alternate). Value 0 => Default Datapath (default) Value 1 => Alternate DataPath
spn_PHY_PCS_REPEATER phy_pcs_repeater Port 0 Bypass the PCS retimer function to provide better latency. However it requires a more clean input clock than in retimer mode
spn_PHY_SYS_INTERFACE phy_sys_interface Port 0 Specify the sytem side interface to be configured for the PHY
spn_PHY_ULL_DATAPATH phy_ull_datapath Port 0 Specify the data path mode to be configured for the PHY
spn_PHY_TX_DISABLE_NO_LPMODE phy_tx_disable_no_lpmode Port 0 Specify tx disable to not be wired to LPMODE pin from the PHY to the cage
spn_GIG_IOV gig_iov Port 0 gig port i/o voltage control on BCM5615 and similar devices
spn_IF_TBI if_tbi Port 0 Force the port into TBI(10-bit interface) mode
spn_BCM5632_MODE bcm5632_mode 0 Set 10G+ stack ports to default to B5632 encapsulation instead of HiGig format

spn_BCM_METER_CLEAR_GE bcm_meter_clear_ge 1 Reset meters for 1000Mb ports during initialization
spn_BCM_METER_CLEAR_XE bcm_meter_clear_xe 1 Reset meters for 10GE ports during initialization
spn_XGXS_PREEMPHASIS xgxs_preemphasis Port (phyrev>2 Fusion/Uni core preemphasis, driver current and pre-driver current values 0-15 (can be changed per-port)

spn_XGXS_PRE_DRIVER_CURRENT xgxs_pre_driver_current Port 0xb Configure the given pre driver current value for applicable XGXS serdes devices.

spn_XGXS_LCPLL xgxs_lcpll Port SAL_BOOT_QUICKTURN?0:1 Fusion core reference clock selection External Clock = 0, Internal LCPLL = 1
spn_LOAD_FIRMWARE load_firmware Port 2 this property is for debug and diagnostic purpose. byte0: 0: not loading WC firmware 1: load from MDIO. default method. 2: load from parallel bus if applicable. Provide fast downloading time byte1: bit 0 0: inform uC not to perform checksum calculation(default). Save ~70ms for WC init time 1: inform uC to perform checksum calculation. byte1: bit 4 0: not to do the FW load verify 1: do the FW load verify.
spn_XGXS_LCPLL_12GBPS xgxs_lcpll_12gbps Port 0 Fusion core LCPLL clock speed selection - 10Gbps = 0, 12Gbps = 1
spn_XGXS_PDETECT_10G xgxs_pdetect_10g Port 1 Unicore 10G parallel detect (10/12 Gbps legacy speed detection)
spn_XGXS_TX_LANE_MAP xgxs_tx_lane_map Port 0x0123 or 0x3210 for Warpcore serdes Remap XGXS tx lanes to desired mapping. See xgxs_rx_lane_map
spn_XGXS_RX_LANE_MAP xgxs_rx_lane_map Port 0x0123 or 0x3210 for Warpcore serdes Remap XGXS rx lanes to desired mapping. Four bits were used for specifying each lane in the format of Lane 0 (bit 15-12), Lane 1 (bit 11-8), lane 2 (bit 7-4), and lane 3 (bit 3-0). For example, to reverse the rx lane mapping in 3, 2, 1, 0 order, set xgxs_rx_lane_map=0x3210. However for Warpcore serdes device, the format is in reversed order, that is, Lane 3 (bit 15-12), Lane 2 (bit 11-8),lane 1 (bit 7-4), and lane 0 (bit 3-0), The example above will be: set xgxs_rx_lane_map=0x0123.
spn_PHY_TX_LANE_MAP phy_tx_lane_map Port 0x3210 - 1-to-1 map Remap tx lanes to desired mapping. See phy_rx_lane_map.
spn_PHY_CHAIN_TX_LANE_MAP_PHYSICAL phy_chain_tx_lane_map_physical Port 0x3210 - 1-to-1 map Remap tx lanes to desired mapping. See phy_chain_rx_lane_map_physical.
spn_PHY_XSW_LANE_MAP phy_xsw_lane_map Port 0x76543210 Configure cross-switch lane mapping. Four bits are used for specifying each lane in the format of lane 0 (bits 3-0), lane 1 (bits 7-4), lane 3 (bits 11-8), etc.
spn_PHY_RX_LANE_MAP phy_rx_lane_map Port 0x3210 - 1-to-1 map Remap tx lanes to desired mapping. The format is in reversed order, that is, Lane 3 (bit 15-12), Lane 2 (bit 11-8),lane 1 (bit 7-4), and lane 0 (bit 3-0)
spn_PHY_CHAIN_RX_LANE_MAP_PHYSICAL phy_chain_rx_lane_map_physical Port 0x3210 - 1-to-1 map Remap tx lanes to desired mapping on applicable PHY devices Format: phy_chain_rx_lane_map_physical[{<phys_port>[<phy:num>]}] = VALUE <phys_port>: Physical port number which is corresponding to a physical lane within a Serdes or an external phy. If ommitted, this applies to all PHYs in the chain. <phy_num>: Serdes or phy number. If ommitted, this applies to all PHYs in the chain (internal/external) where the <phys_port> belongs to. 0 = internal Serdes 1 = the external phy directly attached to Serdes 2 = the external phy attached to phy1 3 = the external phy attached to phy2 etc. VALUE: The format is in reversed order, that is, bit3-0: lane 0 for physical port <phys_port> bit7-4: lane 1 for physical port <phys_port> bit11-8: lane 2 for physical port <phys_port> bit15-12: lane 3 for physical port <phys_port> etc. For Example: phy_chain_rx_lane_map_physical{1.0} = 0x2103 Internal Serdes rx lane map on physical port 1 phy_chain_rx_lane_map_physical{1.1} = 0x0123 rx lane swap for the physical physical port 1 in the innermost external phy
spn_PHY_DIAG_BMP phy_diag_bmp Port Bits [1:0] = 0b01 (log to memory) BCM8806X Support Bits [1:0] = 0b00 - log to UART, 0b01 - log to memory, 0b10 - turn off logging
spn_FCMAP_TRANSCEIVER_HOST_MANAGED fcmap_transceiver_host_managed Port 0 (Host Managed) BCM8806X Support Host managed fiber channel transceiver. Is a Per-Port SOC property. 0 -> Not Host managed (Default) 1->Host Managed.
spn_ESM_SERDES_TX_LANE_MAP esm_serdes_tx_lane_map Port 0x3210 for esm serdes Remap ESM serdes tx lanes to desired mapping. Four bits were used for specifying each lane in the format of Lane 3 (bit 15-12), Lane 2 (bit 11-8), lane 1 (bit 7-4), and lane 0 (bit 3-0). For ex: To reverse the rx lane mapping in 0-1-2-3 order, set esm_serdes_tx_lane_map_core0=0x0123. set esm_serdes_tx_lane_map_core1=0x0123, for core1 and so on
spn_ESM_SERDES_RX_LANE_MAP esm_serdes_rx_lane_map Port 0x3210 for esm serdes Remap ESM serdes rx lanes to desired mapping. Four bits were used for specifying each lane in the format of Lane 3 (bit 15-12), Lane 2 (bit 11-8), lane 1 (bit 7-4), and lane 0 (bit 3-0). For ex: To reverse the rx lane mapping in 0-1-2-3 order, set esm_serdes_rx_lane_map_core0=0x0123. set esm_serdes_rx_lane_map_core1=0x0123, for core1 and so on
spn_ESM_SERDES_MASTER_CLK_SRC esm_serdes_master_clk_src Port 2 Select a serdes for master clock source among/for a group of serdes devices For ex: set esm_serdes_master_clk_src=2, to select 3rd serdes(0,1,->2<-)
spn_ESM_SERDES_DRIVER_CURRENT esm_serdes_driver_current 4 ESM serdes lane TX amplitude control, default value is 4
spn_ESM_SERDES_PRE_DRIVER_CURRENT esm_serdes_pre_driver_current 4 ESM serdes lane TX amplitude control, default value is 4
spn_ESM_SERDES_PRECURSOR_TAP esm_serdes_precursor_tap 0 ESM serdes lane TX fir control to AFE for ESM and PentaCore only, default value is 0
spn_ESM_SERDES_MAIN_TAP esm_serdes_main_tap 40 ESM serdes lane TX fir control to AFE for ESM and PentaCore only, default value is 40
spn_ESM_SERDES_POSTCURSOR_TAP esm_serdes_postcursor_tap 7 ESM serdes lane TX fir control to AFE for ESM and PentaCore only, default value is 7

spn_SERDES_LANE_CONFIG serdes_lane_config Port 0 serdes PMD lane configurations. suffixes and property values for each suffix: - dfe: on|off|lp - media_type: backplane|copper|optics - unreliable_los: 0|1 - cl72_auto_polarity_en: 0|1 - cl72_restart_timeout_en: 0|1 - channel_mode: force_nr|force_er for example, for logical port ce0, you can specify serdes_lane_config_dfe_ce0=on this will be implying that for logical port ce0 DFE is on
spn_PORT_LP_TX_PRECODER port_lp_tx_precoder Port 0 has the link partner enabled pre-coding on its TX side in other words - enable the decoding on my RX side. the configuration is per logical port. to enable the feature on my rx, the property value should be "enable". to disable the feature on my rx, the property value should be "disable". for example: port_lp_tx_precoder_ce0=enable will imply that precoding is enabled on TX side of the link partner of logical port ce0 and so decoding is enabled on RX of logical port ce0.
spn_PORT_TX_PAM4_PRECODER port_tx_pam4_precoder Port 0 is the precoding enabled on TX side the configuration is per logical port. to enable precoding, the property value should be "enable". to disable precoding, the property value should be "disable". for example: port_tx_pam4_precoder_ce0=enable will imply that precoding is enabled on TX side of logical port ce0
spn_SERDES_TX_TAPS serdes_tx_taps serdes_tx_taps to specify either 3 taps or 6 taps, in nrz or pam4 signalling mode. this config is per logical port. the taps are decimal numbers, positive or negative, separated by a colon ":". the first parameter will specify whether the Tx params are suitable for nrz or pam4 signaling mode. the order will be as follows: For 3 taps mode: serdes_tx_taps_<port>=signaling_mode:pre:main:post For example, for ce3 in 3 taps mode, pre=8, main=50, post=12, that will be working in nrz mode, The config will be serdes_tx_taps_ce3=nrz:8:50:12 For 6 taps mode: serdes_tx_taps_<port>=signaling_mode:pre:main:post:pre2:post2:post3 For example, for ce9 that needs to config 6 taps mode, pre1=-10, main=60, post1=8, pre2=2, post2=-4, post3=3, that will be working in pam4 mode, serdes_tx_taps_ce9=pam4:-10:60:8:2:-4:3 if this config is not specified, then SDK will use its own default tx taps value.
spn_SERDES_CORE_TX_POLARITY_FLIP_PHYSICAL serdes_core_tx_polarity_flip_physical 0 this config is per PM Core serdes_core_tx_polarity_flip_physical{phys_port} phys_port will be the first physical port on that core bit 0 represents the logical lane 0 tx flip bit 1 represents the logical lane 1 tx flip, etc... for example serdes_core_tx_polarity_flip_physical{5}=0xc5 the core which is used by physical port 5 have lane 0,2,6 and 7 tx flipped
spn_SERDES_CORE_RX_POLARITY_FLIP_PHYSICAL serdes_core_rx_polarity_flip_physical 0 this config is per PM Core serdes_core_rx_polarity_flip_physical{phys_port} bit 0 represents the logical lane 0 rx flip bit 1 represents the logical lane 1 rx flip, etc... serdes_core_rx_polarity_flip_physical{9}=0x38 the core which is used by physical port 5 have lane lane 3,4 and 5 rx flipped
spn_L1_PRIMARY_CLK_RECOVERY_PORT L1_primary_clk_recovery_port 0 Selects the primary L1 clock recovery port. Choose a non-cpu port that does not have an external phy.
spn_L1_BACKUP_CLK_RECOVERY_PORT L1_backup_clk_recovery_port 0 Selects the backup L1 clock recovery port. Choose a non-cpu port that does not have an external phy.
spn_PBMP_VALID pbmp_valid 0 BCM5665L and BCM5666L support The BCM5665L and BCM5666L device IDs are 0x5665, same as the BCM5665. However, these devices do not support the upper 24 FE ports. The following property must be used to invalidate them.
spn_LLA_TESTS lla_tests 0 (No patterns selected) Configure the memory tests run during BCM5670 initialization (using MT_PAT_* flags)
spn_STACK_ENABLE stack_enable 0
spn_STACK_SIMPLEX stack_simplex 1
spn_STACK_CPU_PRIORITY stack_cpu_priority 0 Stack master priority for stacking examples.
spn_LOSSLESS_MODE lossless_mode 0 By default, 5670 will be configured to accept the maximum number of packets per port, but may drop them if resources are oversubscribed due to activity from other ports. If lossless mode is enabled, 5670 will instead be configured to accept packets only if sufficient processing resources are guaranteed for all ports. This may decrease overall throughput, but no accepted packets will be dropped.
spn_MIRROR_5670_MODE mirror_5670_mode 0 Allow a BCM5675 fabric device to mirror using the same method as a BCM5670 fabric.
spn_CORE_CLOCK_12G core_clock_12G 0 Configure a BCM5675 fabric device to to operate with a 12G core clock.
spn_MMU_HOL_JITTER mmu_hol_jitter 0 BCM5675 HOL blocking avoidance mode (jitter and hysteresis) Set this to 1 to enable jitter for comparing low cell/packet count thresholds
spn_MMU_HOL_HYSTERESIS mmu_hol_hysteresis 0 Set this to 1 to enable hysteresis with recommended default low thresholds
spn_PHY_RESET_TIMEOUT phy_reset_timeout PHY_RESET_TIMEOUT_USEC Specify IEEE MII reset timeout value for copper PHY devices
spn_I2C_NVRAM_SKIP i2c_nvram_skip 0 24c64 EEPROM and XFP share the same I2C slave address. Set this to 1 to treat the device found at this slave address as XFP.
spn_I2C_HCLK_SKIP i2c_hclk_skip 0 PCF8574 lpt2 and LTC4258 poe3 share the same I2C slave address. Set this to 1 to treat the device found at this slave address as POE.
spn_I2C_POE_POWER i2c_poe_power 0 PD63000 init power setting. Set this to 1 for 100W; otherwise default of 37W is used.
spn_I2C_TIMEOUT_USEC i2c_timeout_usec I2C_TIMEOUT The maximum wait time for a I2C transaction to complete in interrupt-driven mode.
spn_PHY_XAUI_TX_LANE_SWAP phy_xaui_tx_lane_swap Port 0 Swap XGXS device tx lane 0, 1, 2, 3 to lane 3, 2, 1, 0 on 10G PHYs
spn_PHY_XAUI_RX_LANE_SWAP phy_xaui_rx_lane_swap Port FALSE Swap XGXS device rx lane 0, 1, 2, 3 to lane 3, 2, 1, 0 on 10G PHYs

spn_SERDES_RXAUI_MODE serdes_rxaui_mode Port 0 specify rxaui mode
spn_SERDES_USE_PROXY_REMOVAL serdes_use_proxy_removal Port 1 To disable the logic of proxy removal
spn_SERDES_PCS_20G_ALIGNMENT_MARKER_RESERVED serdes_pcs_20g_alignment_marker_reserved Port 0 To set customers specific alignment marker
spn_PHY_XAUI_TX_POLARITY_FLIP phy_xaui_tx_polarity_flip Port 0 Flip PHY lane TX polarity on applicable serdes devices Format: phy_xaui_tx_polarity_flip_logicalPort = VALUE VALUE: 1 - Flip TX polarity. 0 - Do not flip TX polarity. Each bit represents one lane. Logical lane 0 is the right most bit. Example: phy_xaui_tx_polarity_flip_xe10 = 0x5 Flip TX polarity on logical lane 0 and logical lane 2 in internal serdes. phy_xaui_tx_polarity_flip_ce0 = 0x104 TX polarity flip lanes: Lane 2 of first quad, Lane 0 of the third quad. For TSCe12, which has three quads for a logical port, the right most nibble represents the first TSCe4 quad while middle nibble represents the second (middle) TSCe4 quad.
spn_PHY_XAUI_RX_POLARITY_FLIP phy_xaui_rx_polarity_flip Port 0 Flip PHY lane RX polarity. Detail see phy_xaui_tx_polarity_flip for values
spn_PHY_TX_POLARITY_FLIP phy_tx_polarity_flip Port 0 Flip PHY lane TX polarity on applicable ext PHY devices Format: phy_tx_polarity_flip_logicalPort = VALUE VALUE: 1 - Flip TX polarity. 0 - Do not flip TX polarity. Each bit represents one lane. For Example: phy_tx_polarity_flip_ce0 = 0x5 Flip TX polarity on the first and third lane of ce0 on external phy The polarity info of one core needs to be given in a signle command.
spn_PHY_RX_POLARITY_FLIP phy_rx_polarity_flip Port 0 Flip PHY lane RX polarity on applicable ext PHY devices Detail see phy_tx_polarity_flip.
spn_PHY_CHAIN_TX_POLARITY_FLIP_PHYSICAL phy_chain_tx_polarity_flip_physical Port 0 Flip PHY lane TX polarity on applicable PHY devices Format: phy_chain_tx_polarity_flip_physical[{<phys_port>.<phy:num>}] = VALUE <phys_port>: Physical port number which is corresponding to a physical lane within a Serdes or an external phy. <phy_num>: Serdes or phy number. 0 = internal Serdes 1 = the external phy directly attached to Serdes 2 = the external phy attached to phy1 3 = the external phy attached to phy2 etc. VALUE: 1 - Flip TX polarity. 0 - Do not flip TX polarity. Should be a 1-bit VALUE For Example: phy_chain_tx_polarity_flip_physical{1.0} = 1 Internal Serdes TX polarity flip is enabled on physical port 1 phy_chain_tx_polarity_flip_physical{1.1} = 1 TX polarity flip is enabled for the physical port 1 in the innermost external phy This format does not applicable for Gearbox mode and Reverse Gearbox mode external Phys. Use phy_tx/rx_polarity_flip instead.
spn_PHY_CHAIN_RX_POLARITY_FLIP_PHYSICAL phy_chain_rx_polarity_flip_physical Port 0 Flip PHY lane RX polarity on applicable PHY devices Detail see phy_chain_tx_polarity_flip_physical.
spn_PHY_PCS_TX_POLARITY_FLIP phy_pcs_tx_polarity_flip Port 0 Flip PCS lane TX polarity. See phy_xaui_tx_polarity_flip for values
spn_PHY_PCS_RX_POLARITY_FLIP phy_pcs_rx_polarity_flip Port 0 Flip PCS lane RX polarity. See phy_xaui_tx_polarity_flip for values
spn_ESM_SERDES_TX_POLARITY_FLIP esm_serdes_tx_polarity_flip Port 0 Flip ESM serdes lane TX polarity. Each lane is represented by a single bit. For ex: Bit0 represents Lane0, Bit1 represents Lane1 value of 0x0001 - Flip TX polarity on lane 0. value of 0x0002 - Flip TX polarity on lane 1. value of 0x0004 - Flip TX polarity on lane 2. value of 0x0008 - Flip TX polarity on lane 3. value of 0x000f - Flip TX polarity on lane 3,2,1,0.
spn_ESM_SERDES_RX_POLARITY_FLIP esm_serdes_rx_polarity_flip Port 0 Flip ESM serdes lane RX polarity. Each lane is represented by a single bit. For ex: Bit0 represents Lane0, Bit1 represents Lane1 value of 0x0001 - Flip RX polarity on lane 0. value of 0x0002 - Flip RX polarity on lane 1. value of 0x0004 - Flip RX polarity on lane 2. value of 0x0008 - Flip RX polarity on lane 3. value of 0x000f - Flip TX polarity on lane 3,2,1,0.
spn_CX4_TO_HIGIG cx4_to_higig Port FALSE Transform CX4 pinout to HiGig pinout on 5650x/5660x
spn_10G_IS_CX4 10g_is_cx4 Port TRUE Set serdes device CX4 mode or HiGig mode for 10G speed. Value TRUE is CX4 mode, FALSE is HiGig mode.
spn_FORCE_OPTRXLOSLVL force_optrxloslvl Port TRUE Control Active Laser Loss of light level.
spn_FORCE_OPTTXENBLVL force_opttxenblvl Port FALSE The following optical controls manage to force various PHY signal on BCM8703/4/5 Control Active Optical Enable output level.
spn_FORCE_OPTTXRSTLVL force_opttxrstlvl Port TRUE Control Active Optical Reset output level.
spn_FORCE_OPTBIASFLTLVL force_optbiasfltlvl Port TRUE Control Active Laser Bias Fault level.
spn_FORCE_OPTTEMPFLTLVL force_opttempfltlvl Port TRUE Control Active Temperature level.
spn_FORCE_OPTPRFLTLVL force_optprfltlvl Port TRUE Control Active Laser Power Fault level.
spn_FORCE_OPTTXFLLVL force_opttxfllvl Port TRUE Control Active TX fault level.
spn_FORCE_OPTRXFLTLVL force_optrxfltlvl Port TRUE Control Active RX fault level.
spn_FORCE_OPTTXONLVL force_opttxonlvl Port TRUE Control Active TX on level.
spn_BYPASS_MCU bypass_mcu 0 BCM5665 family debug mode - bypass MCU, allows diagnostics such as loopback to be run without initializing the MCU (but requires small packet sizes and counts).
spn_MDIO_EXTERNAL_MASTER mdio_external_master 0 Allow external MDIO master access. Otherwise, the switch device is the MDIO master.
spn_PHY_LED1_MODE phy_led1_mode Port 0 Per-port phy LED control values (currently only used by 546x phy driver) see 546x phy data sheets: ledN_mode are LED selector values from phy reg 0x1x[011101, 01110] led_ctrl is phy reg 0x1x[01001]

spn_PHY_LED_SELECT phy_led_select Port 0 select the multi-color LED display pattern on 546x phy device.
spn_PHY_LED_LINK_SPEED_MODE phy_led_link_speed_mode Port 0 Any LED programmed to linkspd(0) or linkspd(1) indicate the link and speed status of the copper interface. The phy has a feature that allows different interpretations of speed and link based on linkspd(0) and linkspd(1). Use this config to select one of the following modes- DEFAULT(0), LINK_LED_MODE(1) & LINK_SPEED_MODE(2)
spn_PHY_LED3_OUTPUT_DISABLE phy_led3_output_disable Port 0 Control the behavior of an LED in the phy to access the TOP_MISC_SPARE_REG_0 to set bit 1 for LOS signal. Need to set bit 1 in this reg on the first port of the chip.
spn_PHY_FIBER_DETECT phy_fiber_detect Port 0 Per-port control of fiber signal detection (for 546x phys) 0 use the phy's default as signal detect 1 use PECL SD as signal detect (default on 5461) 4 use LED4 as signal detect (default on 5464) 10 use EN_10B as signal detect Negating value treats signal detect as loss of signal without needing an external inverter on the board

spn_L2DELETE_CHUNKS l2delete_chunks L2_MEM_CHUNKS_DEFAULT L2 table is DMAed into memory to search for entries to delete when no hardware assists are available. DMA is done in smaller parts to minimize memory use. Must be port of 2.
spn_VLANDELETE_CHUNKS vlandelete_chunks VLAN_MEM_CHUNKS_DEFAULT Size of chunks to read at once while iterating over VLAN XLATE memory
spn_FILTER_RESIZE filter_resize 0 BCM5665 family filter sizes The FE port filters on 5665/50/55 may be configured for two mask/rule sizes 256 rules and 16 masks (default) 128 rules and 24 masks Use this to select the 128/24 configuration for the chip.
spn_MMU_XQ_WEIGHT mmu_xq_weight 1 Spread the XQs across all CoSqs as dictated by the weight properties. This will allow use of all CoSqs. However, if some CoSqs are later disabled, the XQs allocated here to those disabled CoSQs will be unavailable for use. This property configures all CoSq identically. To specify the value for a single CoSq, use the suffix "_cos#". A CoSq-specific value will override an generic property value.
spn_MMU_XQ_AGING mmu_xq_aging 0 Configure per-XQ packet aging for the various CoSQs. The shortest age allowed by H/W is 250 microseconds. The longest age allowed is 7.162 seconds (7162 msec). The maximum ratio between the longest age and the shortest(nonzero) age is 7:2. This property configures all CoSq identically. To specify the value for a single CoSq, use the suffix "_cos#". A CoSq-specific value will override an generic property value.
spn_PBMP_XPORT_XE pbmp_xport_xe 0 On 568xx devices, the XPORT block defaults to XE ports. Uncomment the following line to change all ports to HG ports. A specific bitmap may be provided to select some XE and some HG ports, with the set bits initialized to HG ports. Note that HG and XE ports may be exchanged through the bcm_port_encap_set API.
spn_PBMP_XPORT_GE pbmp_xport_ge 0 Some BCM56xxx devices, such as the BCM568xx series, allow the XPORTs to be configured as XE, HG, and GE ports. XPORTs set in this bitmap will be GE ports.
spn_PBMP_XPORT_CPRI pbmp_xport_cpri 0 Some 56xxx device allow certain ports to be configured as cpri radio ports at boot up depending on the hardware capability.
spn_PBMP_ROE_COMPRESSION pbmp_roe_compression 0 Some 56xxx device allow certain ports to be configured as roe ports.This indicates whether such ports support compression .
spn_PBMP_XPORT_ROE_BACKPLANE pbmp_xport_roe_backplane 0 Some 56xxx device allow certain ports to be classified as roe backplane ports at boot up . These ports connects to the back plane network in radio Ethernet solution
spn_PBMP_XPORT_ROE_MCU pbmp_xport_roe_mcu 0 Some 56xxx device allow certain ports to be classified as roe mcu ports at boot up. These ports connect to the muti protocol control unit in an radio Ethernet solution.
spn_PBMP_XPORT_ROE_BBU pbmp_xport_roe_bbu 0 Some 56xxx device allow certain ports to be classified as roe bbu ports at boot up. These ports connects to the base band unit in a radio Ethernet solution
spn_PBMP_XPORT_ROE_FRONTHAUL pbmp_xport_roe_fronthaul 0 Some 56xxx device allow certain ports to be classified as fronthaul ports at boot up. These ports connects to the front haul network in an radio Ethernet solution
spn_PBMP_GPORT_STACK pbmp_gport_stack String 0x00000006 Uncomment the following line instead to set all GE ports as regular front panel Ethernet ports.
spn_PBMP_LOOPBACK pbmp_loopback String 0x3c000000 pbmp_loopback is used to specify if a HIGIG/HIGIG-LITE port is configured as loopback port Uncomment the following line instead to set all HIGIG/HIGIG-LITE ports as regular front panel Ethernet ports.
spn_PBMP_OVERSUBSCRIBE pbmp_oversubscribe String 0 Port bitmap for ports in oversubscribe mode
spn_OVERSUBSCRIBE_MODE oversubscribe_mode String 0 Config to describe the system Linerate or Oversubscribe mode. 0: Linerate only (default). 1: Oversubscribe mode (all ports will be oversub). 2: Mixed mode. Check device specification for applicability. Port bitmap specified via pbmp_oversubscribe.
spn_PORT_OVERSUBSCRIBE port_oversubscribe Port 0 Config per Physical Port for oversubscription mode. 0: Linerate only(default) 1: Oversubscribe mode. Oversubscribe mode per Physical port takes priority over logical port oversubscribe Port bitmap. This property should be used together with the oversubscribtion mode.
spn_OVERSUBSCRIBE_MIXED_SISTER_25_50_ENABLE oversubscribe_mixed_sister_25_50_enable String 0 Config per device can support 25/50G Mixed Sister Speed port config. 0: 25/50G mixed-sister port config disable per device(default). 1: 25/50G mixed-sister port config enable per device. This property should be used together with the oversubscribe mode.
spn_OVERSUB_SPEED_GROUP_CONSOLIDATION_ENABLE oversub_speed_group_consolidation_enable String 0 Config the capability of speed group consolidation. 0: indicate to disable the capability of speed group consolidation in OS mode(default). 1: indicate to enable capability of speed group consolidation in OS mode. This property should be used together with the oversubscribe mode.
spn_PBMP_LINKPHY pbmp_linkphy String 0 Port bitmap for ports in LinkPHY channelization mode For BCM56450 the ports in blocks [27,32,33,34] and [28,29,30,31] can be member of this port bitmap. For example, to set ports [27,32,33,34] in LinkPHY channelization mode set pbmp_linkphy=0x708000000
spn_PBMP_LINKPHY_ONE_STREAM_PER_SUBPORT pbmp_linkphy_one_stream_per_subport String 0 Port bitmap for ports in LinkPHY channelization mode supporting only one stream per subport for all its subports For BCM56260. For example, to configure port 1 such that all its subports will support only one stream set pbmp_linkphy_one_stream_per_subport=0x00000002
spn_PBMP_SKIP_DEFAULT_LLS pbmp_skip_default_lls String 0 Port bitmap for skipping SDK default LLS tree creation mode. In this mode, the application must create a LLS tree for each port. Note:On BCM56850/BCM56860, the creation of default LLS trees will be skipped when port bitmap spn_PBMP_SKIP_DEFAULT_LLS is non-zero. User should enable MMU traffic for each port with bcmPortControlMmuTrafficEnable if use this mode.

spn_MMU_FLOW_FANIN mmu_flow_fanin MMU_FLOW_FANIN Number of simultaneous senders to each port for flow control purposes
spn_MMU_RED_DROP_PERCENT mmu_red_drop_percent MMU_RED_DROP_PERCENT Percentage of per-port/per-cos packets used before red packets will be dropped
spn_MMU_YELLOW_DROP_PERCENT mmu_yellow_drop_percent MMU_YELLOW_DROP_PERCENT Percentage of per-port/per-cos packets used before yellow packets will be dropped
spn_MMU_STATIC_BYTES mmu_static_bytes MMU_STATIC_BYTES Per-port/per-cos static reserved limit. Rounded up from bytes to next cell size. Remaining cells are put in dynamic pool. If 0, then mmu_static_percent is used.
spn_MMU_STATIC_PERCENT mmu_static_percent MMU_STATIC_PERCENT Percentage of per-port/per-cos cells to use as static reserved limit. Remaining cells are put in dynamic pool. Only used if mmu_static_bytes is 0.
spn_MMU_RESET_BYTES mmu_reset_bytes MMU_RESET_BYTES (1536 * 2) offset from dynamic cell set limits for reset (enable) limits. Rounded up from bytes to next cell size.
spn_MMU_OVERCOMMIT mmu_overcommit MMU_OVERCOMMIT Non-stack port overcommit factor for dynamic pool
spn_MMU_OVERCOMMIT_STACK mmu_overcommit_stack MMU_OVERCOMMIT_STACK Stack port overcommit factor for dynamic pool

spn_EXT_L2_ACL_TABLE_POLICY_WIDTH ext_l2_acl_table_policy_width 0 288-bit external L2 ACL table policy width(multiples of 35 bits). Allowed values are 1, 2, 3, 4, 6
spn_EXT_L2_ACL_TABLE_SCACHE_SIZE ext_l2_acl_table_scache_size 0xffffffff Number of entries in the 288-bit external L2 ACL table to reserve for use as warm-start scache. If a value is not specified, no entries are reserved, and the regular external scache is used for level-2 warm start. If a value is specified, that number of entries are reserved for use as the level-2 warm start scache. If the value specified is 0, an optimal number of reserved entries is calculated such that the reserved space will hold all usable entries.

spn_HIGIG2_MULTICAST_VLAN_RANGE higig2_multicast_vlan_range 4096 Multicast ranges The HiGig2 header format concatenates the broadcast, multicast, and IP multicast indices into one generic multicast index. The mapping between the individual indices and the combined index is specified by these. The default values are indicated. This value sets the allowed range of broadcast indices in the HiGig2 header for stack ports.

Set to 1, Burst will be configured for child of gport node. Set to 0 (default),Burst will be configured for gport node.

On BCM5682x and BCM5672x, the three modes available are: 0 - normal operation 1 - Skip L3 switch logic 2 - Skip L3 and FP switch logic On BCM56960, the switch latency bypass modes availabe are: 0 - normal operation 1 - balanced latency L2 + L3 2 - low latency L2 3 - EFP Bypass

spn_DPORT_MAP_ENABLE dport_map_enable TRUE Enable diag shell port mapping. Port names will be assigned in dport order, and the BCM shell will list multiple ports in dport order regardless of the internal port numbering.
spn_DPORT_MAP_INDEXED dport_map_indexed TRUE Port names for each port type (fe, ge, etc.) will increment by one starting at zero, e.g. if a switch has four xe ports with dport numbers 24, 25, 26, and 27, they will be named xe0, xe1, xe2, and xe3. In non-indexed mode the ports would be named xe24, xe25, xe26, and xe27.
spn_DPORT_MAP_DIRECT dport_map_direct FALSE Traditionally, specifying a raw number instead of a port name in the diag shell will be parsed as if port numbers are counted from 1 up to the number of enabled ports. Typically this would mean that for a gigabit switch, port 1 would correspond to ge0, and so forth. Setting this flag causes raw port numbers to be parsed as internal port numbers.
spn_DPORT_MAP_PORT dport_map_port Port -1 Map dport number <dport> to internal port number <port>. dport_map_port_<port>=<dport>
spn_PORTMON_INTERVAL portmon_interval 0 Interval (in usecs) at which the port monitor thread will run. The port monitor can be used to handle workarounds which are required only with specific equipment configurations.
spn_SERDES_SHADOW_DRIVER serdes_shadow_driver Port FALSE Select whether to always attach the corresponding Serdes shadow driver for Raptor and Raven devices. Note that when deciding which driver to attach, MDIO accesses are also verified independently and checked for corruption. If corruption is detected, the shadow driver is attached regardless of this property. To always attach the shadow driver for a port: serdes_shadow_driver_<port>=1

spn_PORTMAP portmap Port String Specifies the Logical to physical port mapping and bandwidth allocation. portmap_<port>=<physical port number>:<bandwidth in Gb> [:<OSG.0xf - Oversub Speed Group>][:<phy lane config or number of lanes per port or i - inactive port or m - management port>][:<i - inactive port>] [:<queue config>]. Applicable to BCM56840, BCM56740, BCM56850 and BCM56960 device family. portmap_<port>=<physical port number>:<bandwidth in Gb> [:<phy lane config>][:<fallback phy for 100G auto-negotiation>] [:<queue config>][:i - inactive port or m - management port or l - lanes>]. [:<number of lanes for management or Front-panel and HiGig port>] :l option applies only to BCM56860 and cannot be used for inactive ports i.e. cannot be used with :i. spn_PORTGROUP portgroup Port Specifies the number of lanes used by each port in the flex port group. portgroup_<port group>=<number of lanes>. Applicable to BCM566xx and BCM565xx device family Example: portgroup_<port_group> = 1 - Lane independent mode. Each lane is an independent port, for qsgmii the valid speeds are 10/100/1000M, 2.5G. portgroup_<port_group> = 4 - For QSGMII, it means only lane 0 and lane 4 are valid ports that can operate at 10/100/1000M, 2.5G speeds. Lanes 1,2,3 and 5,6,7 are disabled for QSGMII.

spn_BCM53400_INIT_PORT_CONFIG bcm53400_init_port_config 1 Greyhound(bcm 53400) could support varities of port configurations including SKU options and flexible port configuration in TSCx for some SKUs. SKU options and flexible port configuration on TSCx could be configured via bcm53400_init_port_config=<sku option> and the extended suffix tsc[x]. i.e. bcm53400_init_port_config_tsc<# of TSC 0-5> = <SINGLE/XAUI/RXAUI> SINGLE: Initialize 4 GE/XE ports in TSCx. XAUI: Initialize 1 XAUI port in TSCx. RXAUI: Initialize 2 RXAUI ports in TSCx. Note: The Value or String will be valid only when the configurations (sku options and port configurations in TSCx) are listed in the Data sheet.

spn_CONFIG_QUEUE config_queue 0 This configuration allows specification/override source queue config. Valid only on BCM 8803x series. The parameter is per queue so has to be used in conjunction with Queue id The value is comma seperated set of following parameters in a single line {max_pages},{de1_threshold},{de2_threshold}, {fc_treshold},{min_data_pages},{min_hdr_pages} Example: config_queue100=100,80,75,60,10,10

The value is a comma seperated list of Client calendar entries Each entry ranges from 0-6, 6 specifies that slot is to be skipped Maximum number of entries is 255

The value is a comma seperated list of Port calendar entries Each entry ranges from 0-51, -1 specifies that slot is to be skipped Maximum number of entries is 255

spn_TX_FIFO_SIZE tx_fifo_size 0 This configuration allows override for PT Port FIFO Allocation. Valid only on BCM 8803x series. This is typically per port configuration, unless all the ports are the same type Each entry is the number of 32B pages, There is a total of 102 such pages These are typically allocated to each port according to the speed SDK automatically allocates if this parameter is omitted

spn_TXPI_SDM_SCHEME txpi_sdm_scheme Port 0 TX Phase Interpolator SDM (Sigma-Delta Modulator) scheme type for Portmacro core: 0 - 1st order scheme with floor. It follows the traditional TXPI SDM implementation. 1 - 1st order scheme with rounding. It is a new implementation that supposed to solve frequent updates introduced by the 1st order floor implementation. 2 - 2nd order scheme with rounding. It is a new implementation that supposed to solve the issue of low frequency phase nose introduced by the 1st order implementation.

spn_BFD_SESSION_DOWN_EVENT_ON_CREATE bfd_session_down_event_on_create 0 If this config property is enabled (set to 1), there would be a state change event (State would be down for the endpoint) received after the session is created if we do not receive any packets from the peer within detection_multiplier * 1 seconds. Default value is 0 (disabled)
spn_BFD_USE_ENDPOINT_ID_AS_DISCRIMINATOR bfd_use_endpoint_id_as_discriminator 0 Enable/Disable the configuration of using endpoint index itself as local discriminator for BFD endpoints.If the config property is enabled (set to 1), any value passed in local_discriminator field in endpoint info will be ignored and endpoint index would be used instead. The default value of the config property is 0 (disabled)
spn_BFD_REMOTE_DISCRIMINATOR bfd_remote_discriminator 0 If the config property is enabled (set to 1), configuring remote discriminator value is always same, not overriding with the learned BFD My discriminator value. The default value of the config property is 0 (disabled)
spn_BFD_CONTROL_PLANE_INDEPENDENCE bfd_control_plane_independence 1 If the config property is enabled by default (set to 1), if bfd_control_plane_independence is 0, Fw transmit BFD packets with C bit 0, otherwise C bit 1. The default value of the config property is 1 (enabled)

spn_PORT_EGRESS_SCHEDULER_CONFGURATION port_egress_scheduler_confguration 0 port egress scheduler configuration. Supported on 88640 device 0: OFFP port scheduler Configuration A. 1: OFFP port scheduler Configuration B..
spn_PORT_EGRESS_RECYCLING_SCHEDULER_CONFIGURATION port_egress_recycling_scheduler_configuration Port egress recycling scheduler configuration. Supported on 88640 and 88650 device 0: Strict Priority Scheduler. 1: Round Robin Scheduler.
spn_DTM_FLOW_MAPPING_MODE_REGION dtm_flow_mapping_mode_region 1 this property is prefixed by the core (core<id>) and region number ("</em>#"). The value that is assigned to this property configures the region mode 0: queue connectors only (InterDigitated = FALSE, OddEven = TRUE) 1: queue connectors, SE (InterDigitated =TRUE, OddEven = TRUE) 2: queue connectors, SE (InterDigitated =TRUE, OddEven = FALSE)
spn_DTM_FLOW_NOF_REMOTE_CORES_REGION dtm_flow_nof_remote_cores_region this property is prefixed by the core id (core#) and region number ("</em>#"). The value that is assigned to this property configures the number of symmetric connections in E2E scheme
spn_DTM_QUEUE_MAPPING_MODE_REGION dtm_queue_mapping_mode_region this property is prefixed by the region number ("_#"). The value that is assigned to this property configures the queue region mode 0: queue region corresponding to connector region with attribute InterDigitated = FALSE 1: queue region corresponding to connector region with attribute InterDigitated = TRUE
spn_PORT_NIF_TYPE port_nif_type Following properties are valid on Petra only
spn_FABRIC_DEVICE_MODE fabric_device_mode String SINGLE_STAGE_FE2 SINGLE_STAGE_FE2, MULTI_STAGE_FE2, MULTI_STAGE_FE13, or REPEATER
spn_IS_DUAL_MODE is_dual_mode FALSE Specify Single (0) or Dual (1) context mode

spn_FABRIC_LINK_FIFO_SIZE_TX fabric_link_fifo_size_tx Specify fabric FIFO depth in TX stage
spn_FABRIC_LOCAL_ROUTING_ENABLE fabric_local_routing_enable 0 Whether local routing from FE1 to FE3 is enabled For generations before Ramon, this SoC property is used without suffix and enables local routing for Unicast traffic only. For Ramon: - to enable local routing for Unicast traffic, use fabric_local_routing_enable_uc - to enable local routing for Multicast traffic, use fabric_local_routing_enable_mc - to enable local routing for both Unicast and Multicast traffic, use fabric_local_routing_enable
spn_SYSTEM_CONTAINS_MULTIPLE_PIPE_DEVICE system_contains_multiple_pipe_device 1 Whether there is a device in multi-pipe mode in system

spn_SYSTEM_IS_DUAL_MODE_IN_SYSTEM system_is_dual_mode_in_system FALSE Whether there is a device in the in dual mode system.
spn_SYSTEM_IS_SINGLE_MODE_IN_SYSTEM system_is_single_mode_in_system FALSE Whether there is a device in the in single mode system.
spn_SYSTEM_IS_FE600_IN_SYSTEM system_is_fe600_in_system FALSE Whether there is an FE600 device in the system.
spn_SYSTEM_IS_PETRA_B_IN_SYSTEM system_is_petra_b_in_system TRUE Whether there is a Petra B device in the system.
spn_SYSTEM_IS_ARAD_IN_SYSTEM system_is_arad_in_system TRUE Whether there is a Arad or Arad Plus device in the system.
spn_SYSTEM_REF_CORE_CLOCK system_ref_core_clock 250 225 - 666 System reference core clock. If there are FE600 devices in the system it must match their frequency. If there are Peter-A devices in the system it must match their frequency or 2/3 of their frequency
spn_FABRIC_MERGE_CELLS fabric_merge_cells FALSE BCM88X4X has a mode to send successive 128B cell on the link. The BCM88X5X can merge this to a single 256B that is processed more efficiently. This mode is set if all VSC128 link are sourced by BCM88X4X.
spn_FABRIC_MULTICAST_MODE fabric_multicast_mode String DIRECT DIRECT or INDIRECT. Indirect mode is used when the maximal FAP module ID is higher than 127. In this case the per-multicast destination IDs bitmap doesn't represent module IDs, rather FAP group IDs, or internal FAP IDs.
spn_MC_TABLE_ENABLE_TDM_PRIORITY mc_table_enable_TDM_priority 0 The multicast table access can be configured to work at a round robin between all requestors or to give priority to the secondary pipe when used for TDM. 0 - use round robin mode between all requesting queries when accessing table. 1 - use strict priority to secondary pipe, to be used in TDM/Non-TDM pipe splitting.
spn_FABRIC_LOAD_BALANCING_MODE fabric_load_balancing_mode String NORMAL_LOAD_BALANCE Select load balancing mode: NORMAL_LOAD_BALANCE, DESTINATION_UNREACHABLE, or BALANCED_INPUT
spn_FABRIC_MAC_BUCKET_FILL_RATE fabric_mac_bucket_fill_rate 0 Number of good cells that add a token to the bucket. Value is set to 2^fabric_mac_bucket_fill_rate. Range valid for BCM88750: 0-11
spn_FABRIC_CELL_FORMAT fabric_cell_format Port String VSC256 Per port cell format VSC128 or VSC256
spn_FABRIC_CELL_FIFO_DMA_ENABLE fabric_cell_fifo_dma_enable 0 Enables fabric cell FIFO dma mode
spn_FABRIC_CELL_FIFO_DMA_BUFFER_SIZE fabric_cell_fifo_dma_buffer_size 20480 Size of the host memory stored allocated by the CPU
spn_FABRIC_CELL_FIFO_DMA_TIMEOUT fabric_cell_fifo_dma_timeout 1000 The amount of time in microseconds that passes from the first write by the DMA until a timeout based interrupt is triggered. Value 0 disables timeout based interrupts.
spn_FABRIC_CELL_FIFO_DMA_THRESHOLD fabric_cell_fifo_dma_threshold 2 The number of writes by the DMA until a threshold based interrupt is triggered.
spn_EGRESS_FABRIC_DROP_THRESHOLD_MULTICAST_LOW egress_fabric_drop_threshold_multicast_low Drop multicast best effort according to Delete-FIFO available resources (number of packet descriptors which can be added to Delete-FIFO).
spn_EGRESS_FABRIC_DROP_THRESHOLD_MULTICAST egress_fabric_drop_threshold_multicast Drop multicast according to Delete-FIFO available resources (number of packet descriptors which can be added to Delete-FIFO).
spn_EGRESS_FABRIC_DROP_THRESHOLD_ALL_EXCEPT_TDM egress_fabric_drop_threshold_all_except_tdm Drop all traffic except TDM according to Delete-FIFO available resources (number of packet descriptors which can be added to Delete-FIFO).
spn_EGRESS_FABRIC_DROP_THRESHOLD_ALL egress_fabric_drop_threshold_all Drop all traffic according to Delete-FIFO available resources (number of packet descriptors which can be added to Delete-FIFO).

spn_VCS128_UNICAST_PRIORITY vcs128_unicast_priority 2 Defines the priority for VCS128 unicast cells
spn_FABRIC_OPTIMIZE_PARTIAL_LINKS fabric_optimize_partial_links FALSE If the BCM88750 is connected with links 0 - 11, 16 - 27, 32 - 43, 48 - 59, 64 - 75, 80 - 91, 96 - 107, 112 - 123 (first 12 in every 16 links group), and the secondary switch is used, then its secondary TX FIFOs can use the memory of the unused links, thus increasing their capacity by 33 percent to 144 entries.
spn_FE_MC_ID_RANGE fe_mc_id_range String Set range of MC IDs
spn_SECONDARY_IS_MULTICAST secondary_is_multicast FALSE Map all incoming multicast traffic to the secondary switch
spn_FE_MC_PRIORITY_MAP_ENABLE fe_mc_priority_map_enable FALSE Enable mapping internal multicast priority from priority field.
spn_SRD_TX_DRV_HV_DISABLE srd_tx_drv_hv_disable 1 High voltage driver strap. If 0, connected to 1.4V supply; if 1, connected to 1V mode.
spn_STAG_ENABLE stag_enable Port If True, then Packets coming from this TM Port have a Statistic Tag header. The Statistic Header position is defined globally according to the pb_itm_stag_set API. Relevant only if the header type is TM.
spn_FIRST_HEADER_SIZE first_header_size Port If True, then Packets coming from this TM Port have a first header to strip before any processing. For example, in the Fat Pipe processing a Sequence Number header (2 Bytes) must be stripped. For injected packets, the PTCH Header must be removed (4 Bytes). Units: Bytes. Range: 0 - 63.
spn_POST_HEADERS_SIZE post_headers_size Port 0 If True, then ITMH packets arriving from this port have their header stripped length according to the SOC property
spn_FLOW_CONTROL_TYPE flow_control_type Port String Flow control type: NONE LL: Link-level. CB2: Class-Based Flow Control (2 classes). CB8: Class-Based Flow Control (8 classes).
spn_SNOOP_ENABLE snoop_enable Port If True, then Packets coming from this TM Port are snooped according to the ITMH. Snoop action command
spn_MIRROR_PROFILE mirror_profile Port Inbound mirroring action command (i.e., its profile) for this PP Port. Range: 0 - 15. Relevant only if the header type is not Ethernet.
spn_TM_INGRESS_SHAPING_ENABLE tm_ingress_shaping_enable Port If True, then TM Packets can come with an Ingress Shaping header before the ITMH. Relevant only if the header type is TM.
spn_TM_PPH_PPH_PRESENT_ENABLE tm_pph_pph_present_enable Port If True, then TM Packets can come with a PPH header after the ITMH (the PPH-present bit in the ITMH can be set). Relevant only if the header type is TM.
spn_LOCAL_TO_TM_PORT local_to_tm_port Port bcm local port to BCM88X4X tm port mapping.
spn_LOCAL_TO_PP_PORT local_to_pp_port Port bcm local port to BCM88X4X pp port mapping.
spn_SYSTEM_CELL_FORMAT system_cell_format String System cell format. Allowed values: FCS: Fixed cell size VSC128: Variable cell size 128B
spn_FABRIC_SEGMENTATION_ENABLE fabric_segmentation_enable If TRUE, fabric segmentation will be performed to improve the fabric performance.
spn_SYSTEM_FTMH_LOAD_BALANCING_EXT_MODE system_ftmh_load_balancing_ext_mode String FTMH load balancing mode. Valid values: DISABLED 8B_LB_KEY_8B_STACKING_ROUTE_HISTORY: load balancing key and an 8-bit stacking route history bitmap. 16B_STACKING_ROUTE_HISTORY: stacking route history. STANDBY_MC_LB: supported in ARAD+.
spn_FAP_DEVICE_MODE fap_device_mode String Fap device mode: TM: only traffic management features are enabled. PP: packet processing mode. TDM_OPTIMIZED: TDM Cells traffic mode with an Optimized FTMH Header format. If set, all the devices this device can communicate with must be configured with the same mode. Invalid for ARAD. TDM_STANDARD: TDM Cells traffic mode with a Standard FTMH Header format. In this mode, the device can communicate with devices (other devices should be configured in TM/PP/TDM_STANDARD mode). Invalid for ARAD.
spn_FAP_TDM_BYPASS fap_tdm_bypass String 0 supported on ARAD device. If non 0 TDM packets bypass Queuing is enabled operation when in hybrid mode (i.e both data packets and TDM packets). TDM_OPTIMIZED: TDM Cells traffic mode with an Optimized FTMH Header format. If set, all the devices this device can communicate with must be configured with the same mode. TDM_STANDARD: TDM Cells traffic mode with a Standard FTMH Header format. In this mode, the device can communicate with devices (other devices should be configured in TM/PP/TDM_STANDARD mode).
spn_FAP_TDM_PACKET fap_tdm_packet String 0 if this soc property is 0, configuring ports to TDM packet mode traffic is not allowed.
spn_TDM_SOURCE_FAP_ID_OFFSET tdm_source_fap_id_offset Supported on ARAD devices.Used to support sending TDM (OTN/CBR) packets from multiple FAPs to a FAP which supports a smaller size of such packets. Like when sending packets from Arad to Petra. The packet source FAP ID will be set tothe ID of the source FAP plus the offset specified here. The resulting value needs to be different than all FAP IDs and different then all other source FAP IDs.
spn_SYSTEM_HAS_FAP20 system_has_fap20 If TRUE, fap20 devices exist in the system. This imposes certain limitations on the device behavior (e.g. fabric cells must be fixed size, fap20-compatible fabric header must be used etc.).
spn_SYSTEM_HAS_FAP21 system_has_fap21 If TRUE, fap21 devices exist in the system. This imposes certain limitations on the device behavior (e.g. fabric cells must be fixed size etc.).
spn_SYSTEM_HAS_PETRA_REV_A system_has_petra_rev_a If TRUE, Petra Rev-A devices exist in the system. This imposes certain limitations on the device behavior (e.g. PPH is in Petra-A compatible mode).
spn_SYSTEM_IS_FE1600_IN_SYSTEM system_is_fe1600_in_system FALSE Whether there is an FE1600 device in the system.

spn_EXT_RAM_TYPE ext_ram_type String DRAM type. Values: DDR2/DDR3/GDDR3.
spn_EXT_RAM_PACKET_CRC_ENABLE ext_ram_packet_crc_enable If set, a 16b CRC is appended to the end of the packet in the DRAM (aligned to the last two bytes of a 32B word).
spn_EXT_RAM_BANKS ext_ram_banks Number of Banks.
spn_EXT_RAM_COLUMNS ext_ram_columns Number of DRAM columns. Possible values: 256/512/1024/2048/4096/8192
spn_EXT_RAM_TOTAL_SIZE ext_ram_total_size Summarized DRAM size of all DRAM interfaces. Units: Mbytes.
